Arle comments on Rulue speaking like an old lady, but that because of the way she speaks in Japanese, and that can't really be conveyed in English without going Ye Olde Englishe, which wouldn't really fit. So I looked up really old drink ads and settled on an old Coca Cola ad (1929). It should be popular enough that you can look it up and find its source. Mind you, this is just my take on this conversation. You can go for a different thing, and also change Arle's comment to something else, as long as it's her commenting on Rulue's behavior. Keep in mind that Rulue does drink something.
